    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1644833282" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2354704344570116486">A treasurable guide book for travelers.<br/>Equipped with knowledge, motivation, inspiration and guidance, ‘Crash Lane News’ is a perfect guide book or rather a self help book for travelers to be included in their plan of travelling safety & security. Answering the 'How, What and When', this read is an alternative source of accident news with an attempt to give a traveler advice on how not to become involved in a crash.<br/>The new sections added to the book from The National Highway Traffic Safety Admini</span>
  <span id="freeText2354704344570116486" style="display:none">A treasurable guide book for travelers.<br />Equipped with knowledge, motivation, inspiration and guidance, ‘Crash Lane News’ is a perfect guide book or rather a self help book for travelers to be included in their plan of travelling safety &amp; security. Answering the 'How, What and When', this read is an alternative source of accident news with an attempt to give a traveler advice on how not to become involved in a crash.<br />The new sections added to the book from The National Highway Traffic Safety Administration (NHTSA), The Federal Emergency Management Agency (FEMA), The Federal Motor Carriers Safety Administration (FMCSA), Department of Transportation (DOT) and many more, definitely comes out with an objective to bring out the importance of keeping a notice of weather and traffic density for a well planned trip guarded with well being and safety for travelers in any circumstances.<br />‘Crash Lane News’ is a well researched work in the field of travelling with a gripping narration embedded with some professional suggestions about personal security procedures for a trip, focusing on travel safety, drawing advantage from the examples of safety data put across in a thoughtful manner. This book is a non fiction travel book and is based on real life examples worthy of attention for those who travel for work, pleasure or both. To describe the treasurable knowledge touching every nook and corner of travelling and aspects related to it is beyond mere words. Many awards won by ‘Crash Lane News’ in 2015-2016 speaks volumes about this highly recommended master piece.</span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2385544221?book_show_action=true">May 08, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2385544221" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14090536773228374224">'Crash Lane News' is definitely a must-have for anyone planning a trip, big or small. It doesn't just take into account the important issues that can come up when traveling, but also the things that can easily be forgotten, such as safety equipment or emergency supplies that are useful to have with you just in case. This advice would certainly have come in handy for me when trapped on a coach on a motorway for ten hours after a heavy snowfall. The book is full of a number of great tips for trave</span>
  <span id="freeText14090536773228374224" style="display:none">'Crash Lane News' is definitely a must-have for anyone planning a trip, big or small. It doesn't just take into account the important issues that can come up when traveling, but also the things that can easily be forgotten, such as safety equipment or emergency supplies that are useful to have with you just in case. This advice would certainly have come in handy for me when trapped on a coach on a motorway for ten hours after a heavy snowfall. The book is full of a number of great tips for travelers that is communicated in an interesting way, with great use of charts and diagram, as opposed to long sections of prose.<br /><br />The book shows how aware that travelers need to be when it comes to the information the media is giving them. They need to know that they may not be getting the full picture, as it may not be beneficial to a number of industries to tell tourists not to travel, or to avoid certain areas. 'Crash Lane News' gives the reader the knowledge to know where to look to get the correct information, particularly on the weather, so they don't end up in trouble on the road. An essential read for all those that want to have fun and travel, but want to do so safely.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14090536773228374224" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer3132349845093993">Crash Lane News is a great book for travellers of all kinds. There are suggestions for all kinds of things, some that may seem obvious, but if like me you forget all kinds where the pressure picks up just before you take a trip then this is all kinds of helpful. I don’t think I’ve ever set off on a trip and not forgotten to check something, so this is an invaluable resource for me.<br/><br/>The weather aspect of the book I found even more helpful.   <span id="freeText3132349845093993" style="display:none">Crash Lane News is a great book for travellers of all kinds. There are suggestions for all kinds of things, some that may seem obvious, but if like me you forget all kinds where the pressure picks up just before you take a trip then this is all kinds of helpful. I don’t think I’ve ever set off on a trip and not forgotten to check something, so this is an invaluable resource for me.<br /><br />The weather aspect of the book I found even more helpful. As climate continues to change and weather becomes an even more potent force the recommendations here are a vital tool for travellers all over the US.<br /><br />Safety laws are also covered in the book and I followed up at the website too. I’m not sure if there have been previous editions of the book but having the added resource of double checking the latest changes via the net too is even better. <br /><br />All in all a great book for travellers of all kinds, no matter where in the US you’re setting off from or heading too.<br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('L5mpl1KCtkiHyYDA6TGNVHtVAn6ZBUoGzWttVepKEkF66IH/bWwq39CO3viCcNrireQ/RHWDKRYd+m1m9sOBUQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('9H2wwUdedMyar770kwEAn6PiY3OlyRLoI+d3+wcJxA2hDJipeLDoW83o4Mz4QFcpdVNeSUlPcfjzdnfIG4BXHQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
